Character Changes

Notes:

* Buffs are in blue, Nerfs are in red, quality of life/overhaul/global/engine adjustments are in black. Italics denote the overall changes made to the listed move or new tech/features that have been implemented.

  • - RYU -

    • Attributes:
      • Walk Speed: 0.75 🠚 0.825
      • Walk Acceleration (base/additional): 1/0.1 🠚 1.12/0.11
      • Initial Dash Speed: 1.76 🠚 1.7
      • Run Speed: 1.6 🠚 1.535

      • Initial Jump Velocity: 14.3 🠚 10.725
      • Model Scale Multiplier: 0.98 🠚 1.02
      • Shield Radius: 11.7 🠚 12.3
    • General:
      • Ryu’s horizontal Air Dodge is now an air dash that can be canceled on frame 9
        • Invincibility Frames: 3-19 🠚 4-8
        • Cancel Frame: 9
        • Landing Speed Multiplier: 1 🠚 0.875
        • Airdash GFX added
      • Ryu can now execute a magic series, being able to cancel moves on shield or on hit. Moves lower in the hierarchy can be canceled into those higher in the hierarchy, in the order of:

Light 🠚 Medium 🠚 Heavy 🠚 Command Normal 🠚 Special

  • Light: jab 1, light dtilt, light utilt, nair

  • Medium: jab 2, light ftilt, proximity ftilt, heavy dtilt, fair, uair

  • Heavy: jab 3, heavy jab, heavy utilt, fsmash, up smash, down smash, bair, dair

  • Command Normal: proximity jab, heavy ftilt

  • Special: Hadoken, Tatsumaki Senpukyaku, Shoryuken, Focus Attack, fsmash

  • Jabs 🠚 Tilts / (Dash Attack) 🠚 Smash Attacks / (Aerials) 🠚 Special Moves

  • In addition, jab 1 can cancel into light dtilt and light utilt

  • Moves are subject to “cancel scaling” - if a move is canceled into via magic series, the move will have altered knockback and less damage

  • Ryu now has a meter system

    • Rack up damage to build meter up to a max of 10 levels
      • Ryu will gain a blue star above his head whenever a meter level is gained
    • Meter can be checked by pressing or holding a taunt button at any time; Your current level will be signified by the number of stars above Ryu’s head
      • Added meter bars are now signified by large, blue stars
      • Burned meter bars are now signified by small, transparent stars
    • In training mode, meter can be filled instantly by pressing shield during taunt

    • General:
      • Bayonetta has two recovery uses per airtime
        • Using Afterburner Kick and Witch Twist and whiffing them will use up one resource; hitting either will not use the recovery resource
        • Once Bayonetta runs out of recovery resources, she cannot use Witch Twist or Afterburner Kick again until she lands or grabs ledge. She will gain one resource back if she gets hit
      • Bayonetta can cancel all aerials except down air into jump or specials
        • Down air can be special canceled but not jump canceled
      • Canceling aerials into jump (or canceling forward air 2 into another aerial) will reduce the next aerial’s damage by 2.0%
        • Knockback is compensated for the prorated aerials

  • - KEN -

    • Attributes:
      • Walk Speed: 0.825 🠚 0.875
      • Walk Acceleration (base/additional): 1.1/0.11 🠚 1.2/0.12
      • Initial Dash Speed: 1.936 🠚 1.7
      • Run Speed: 1.76 🠚 1.825
      • Run Acceleration (base/additional): 0.044/0.11 🠚 0.044/0.086
      • Traction: 0.11 🠚 0.105
      • Max Horizontal Jump Speed: 1.3 🠚 1.55
      • Footstool Vertical Jump Multiplier (fullhop/shorthop): 0.8/0.5 🠚 0.825
      • Air Speed: 1.12 🠚 1.1
      • Fall Speed: 1.6 🠚 2.2
      • Fast Fall Speed: 2.24 🠚 2.9
      • Gravity: 0.12 🠚 0.13
      • Initial Jump Velocity: 14.3 🠚 10.725
      • Short Hop Height: 15 🠚 12
      • Model Scale Multiplier: 0.98 🠚 1.02
      • Shield Radius: 11.7 🠚 12.3
    • General:
      • Ken can now execute a magic series, being able to cancel moves on shield or on hit. Moves lower in the hierarchy can be canceled into those higher in the hierarchy, in the order of:

Light 🠚 Medium 🠚 Heavy 🠚 Command Normal 🠚 Special

  • Light: jab 1, light dtilt, light utilt

  • Medium: jab 2, light ftilt, proximity ftilt, heavy dtilt

  • Heavy: heavy ftilt, heavy utilt, proximity jab, heavy jab, fsmash, up smash, down smash

  • Command Normal: Oosoto Mawashi Geri, Nata Otoshi Geri

  • Special: Hadoken, Tatsumaki Senpukyaku, Shoryuken, Focus Attack

  • In addition, jab 1 can be canceled into light up tilt and light down tilt

  • Moves are subject to “cancel scaling” - if a move is canceled into via magic series, the move will have altered knockback and less damage

  • Ken now has a meter system

    • Rack up damage to build meter up to a max of 10 levels
      • Ken will gain a blue star above his head whenever a meter level is gained
    • Meter can be checked by pressing or holding a taunt button at any time; Your current level will be signified by the number of stars above Ken’s head
      • Added meter bars are now signified by large, blue stars
      • Burned meter bars are now signified by small, transparent stars
    • In training mode, meter can be filled instantly by pressing shield during taunt

      • Platdrop FAF: 13 🠚 4
    • General:
      • Terry can now execute a magic series, being able to cancel moves on shield or on hit. Moves lower in the hierarchy can be canceled into those higher in the hierarchy, in the order of:

Light 🠚 Heavy/Command Normal 🠚 Special

  • Light: jab 1, dtilt, nair

  • Heavy Normal: jab 2, jab 3, ftilt, down smash, fsmash, fair, bair, hair, dair

  • Command Normal: utilt, up smash

  • Special: Power Charge, Power Wave, Burn Knuckle, Crack Shoot, Rising Tackle, Power Dunk

  • Terry also has additional target combos:

    • Jab 1 🠚 dtilt, utilt
    • Jab 2 🠚 utilt
    • Smash Attack 🠚 Power Charge

  • Moves are subject to “cancel scaling” - if a move is canceled into via magic series, the move will have altered knockback and less damage

  • Terry now has a meter system

    • Rack up damage to build meter up to a max of 10 levels
      • Added meter levels are signified by a blue star above Terry’s head on meter gain, meter drain will display small transparent stars
    • Meter is gained multiple times throughout the duration of a move; Canceling a move early will reduce the amount of meter gained
    • Specials can be canceled into Power Geyser and Buster Wolf on hit for 6 bars of meter
    • Power Geyser and Buster Wolf can be canceled into each other respectively for an additional 2 bars of meter
    • Specials can be canceled into Triple Geyser by inputting a half-circle forward and Attack/Special for 10 bars of meter
      • Triple Geyser can be canceled into from Power Geyser or Buster Wolf for an additional 6 bars of meter
    • Meter can be checked by pressing or holding a taunt button at any time; Your current level will be signified by the number of stars above Terry’s head
    • In training mode, meter can be filled instantly by pressing shield during taunt
    • The GO! Meter will appear when Terry has at least four bars of meter
